 mujhe pataa nahin aadhaar ke vivaad ko samajhane main madad karti he yaa nahin lekin saajha kar saktaa hum

 Chikungunya is spreading very fast
 chikangunia edies machhar ke kaatane se failane vaali ek sankramak beemaari he
 The symptoms of this disease do not appear immediately after a mosquito bite
 machhar kaatane ke do se teen din baad iskaa sankraman shuru hota he
 Chikugunia is not fatal but if it is not treated in time, it can prove dangerous
 aise main iske lakshan najar aate hi ilaaj shuru kar den taaki isse jude khatre ko taala ja sake
 Symptoms of Chikungunya: 1
 chikangunia kaa sabase pramukh lakshan yah he ki isamen jodon main tej dard hota he
 There is severe pain in the body before fever
 kai baar dard itnaa adhik hota he kimarij kaa bistar se uthanaa mushkilho jaataa he
 2
 chikangunia main tej bukhaar aata he
 Sometimes the temperature even reaches 104 degrees
 bukhaar ke saath thand bhi lagati he
 3
 chikangunia main bukhaar ke baad 3 se 4 din ke andar sharir par laal chakatte pad jate hai
 4
 ulti hona,sirdard hona or mansapeshiyon main khinchaav hona is beemaari ke pramukh lakshan hai
 5
 kai baar ankhen laal ho jaati hai or pani aane lagata he
 In Chikungunya, dryness is also practiced
 chikangunia se bachaav ke upaay1
 Do not let water accumulate anywhere around you
 ruke hue pani main machhar panpate hai
 It is very important to protect yourself from mosquitoes
 raat main sote samay machharadaani kaa istemaal karen
 2
 puure kapade pahanen
 Keep the body covered so that mosquitoes are protected
 3
 Keep the house clean
 ghar ke baahar, gamalon main, bagiche main yaa phir kisi bhi jagah par jahaan pani jamaa ho saktaa he us jagah kii safai karen
 Sprinkle lime where there is dampness
 4
 Spray insecticides so that mosquitoes do not thrive
 chikangunia kaa ilaajaaye sach he ki abhi tak chikangunia kii koi vaxin uplabdh nahi he
 To reduce fever and joint pain, doctors recommend taking paracetamol
 is dauraan jitna ho sake aaraam karen or apane doctor ke sampark main rahen
